Accessibility digest

Requesterpool@jpdev.pro

Score882
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 882, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 297. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 100. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

Classified issues

Issue linkNoText

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 55

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r11, score 20 (Link has no accessible name)
  • Package axe, test link-name, score 15 (Link has no discernible text)
  • Package continuum, test 237, score 20 (a element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name value to be calculated)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_2.H91.A.NoContent, score 16 (Link has an href attribute but no text)
  • Package wave, test e:link_empty, score 16 (Link contains no text)
  • Package tenon, test 57, score 16 (Link has no text inside it)

Issue duplicateID

WCAG: 4.1.1

Score: 49

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r3, score 24 (Element id attribute value is not unique)
  • Package axe, test duplicate-id-aria, score 4 (id attribute used in ARIA or in a label has a value that is not unique)
  • Package axe, test duplicate-id, score 2 (id attribute value is not unique)
  • Package continuum, test 94, score 24 (Element contains an id attribute set to a value that is not unique in the DOM)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_1.F77, score 12 (Duplicate id attribute value)
  • Package ibm, test RPT_Elem_UniqueId, score 16 (Element id attribute value is not unique within the document)

Issue imageNoText

WCAG: 1.1.1

Score: 44

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_1_1.H37, score 12 (img element has no alt attribute)
  • Package ibm, test WCAG20_Img_HasAlt, score 4 (Image has no alt attribute conveying its meaning, or alt="" if decorative)
  • Package wave, test e:alt_missing, score 36 (Text alternative is missing)

Issue spontaneousMotion

WCAG: 2.2.2

Score: 41

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test motion, score 39 (Change of visible content not requested by user)

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 29

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r69, score 14 (Text outside widget has subminimum contrast)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 17 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
  • Package wave, test c:contrast, score 12 (Very low contrast)

Issue contentBeyondLandmarks

WCAG: 1.3.6

Score: 22

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r57, score 16 (Perceivable text content is not included in any landmark)
  • Package axe, test region, score 5 (Some page content is not contained by landmarks)
  • Package ibm, test Rpt_Aria_OrphanedContent_Native_Host_Sematics, score 6 (Content does not reside within an element with a landmark role)

Issue pageLanguage

WCAG: 3.1.1

Score: 14

  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.3_1_1.H57.2, score 4 (html element has no lang or xml:lang attribute)
